            var slotName = "dfpInjectionb364262b4211f351b825";

            googletag.cmd.push(function() {

                var slot = googletag.defineSlot('/' + DFP_networkId + '/' + DFP_sitepage, [[970,30],[970,90],[970,250]], slotName).
                    setTargeting("position","Top1")
                    .setTargeting("pagetype","events")                                        .setCollapseEmptyDiv(true)
                                        ;

                    if(DFP_adTargets){
                        for(var key in DFP_adTargets){
                            slot.setTargeting(key, DFP_adTargets[key]);
                        }
                    }


                    slot.addService(googletag.pubads());


                    var mapping = googletag.sizeMapping().addSize([992, 480], [[970,30],[970,90],[970,250]]).addSize([0, 0], [[320,50]]).build();slot.defineSizeMapping(mapping);

    <h3 class="mtn">

            <span itemprop="name">AT&amp;T Stadium</span>
        </a>

                <span class="listing__location">
            in Arlington        </span>
        
    </h3>

            1 AT&amp;T Way            <br>
